NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE

2113

NOTICES
RISHIVIDYA CONSULTANTS PRIVATE LIMITED
Regd Office:— E3A Rain Tree Apartments, No. 21. Venus Colony, Second Cross, Alwarpet, Chennai-600 018.
NOTICE BY COMPANY OF MEMBERS’ VOLUNTARY WINDING UP AND APPOINTMENT OF LIQUIDATOR
At the Extraordinary General Meeting of the Company duly convened and held at its Registered Office on Wednesday
the 10th day of July 2013 the equity shareholders have passed special resolution for:—
(i)

Voluntary winding up of the company under section 484(1)(b) of the Companies Act. 1956 and for
appointment of Mr. V.S. Ganesan, Chartered Accountant as the Liquidator in terms of Section 490 of the
Companies Act, 1956 and for fixing his remuneration.

(ii)

Anthorizing the Liquidator to do all such acts and deeds as may be necessary for winding up the affairs
of the company and distributing its assets.

Chennai,
26th July 2013.

For Rishividya consultants Private Limited
K. VENKATESAN,
Managing Director.
Form No. 151

The Registrar of Companies, Tamil Nadu, Chennai
I, Mr. V.S. Ganesan, Chartered Accountant, No. 11, Rajan Street, T. Nagar, Chennai-600 017, hereby give notice that
I have been appointed liquidator of M/s Rishividya Consultants Private Limited by resolution of the company dated
10th July. 2013.
Chennai,
26th July 2013.

V.S. GANESAN,
Chartered Accountant.
